YES

********************************************************************************
Proof Outline:

Remains to prove termination of a 3-rules system (3 strict rules).
Reversing the system.
Remains to prove termination of a 3-rules system (3 strict rules).
Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
Remains to prove termination of a 8-rules system (5 strict rules).
Removing 3 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 5-rules system (2 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 51-rules system (6 strict rules).
Removing 5 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 46-rules system (5 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 680-rules system (20 strict rules).
Removing 154 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 526-rules system (11 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 8588-rules system (50 strict rules).
Removing 8060 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 528-rules system (0 strict rules).
QED

Proof:

After renaming modulo the bijection { a ↦ 0, b ↦ 1, c ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 3-rules system (3 strict rules)
{ 0 ⟶ ,
  0 1 ⟶ 1 1 0 0 2 0 ,
  2 2 0 ⟶ }

Reversing the system.
After renaming modulo the bijection { 0 ↦ 0, 1 ↦ 1, 2 ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 3-rules system (3 strict rules)
{ 0 ⟶ ,
  1 0 ⟶ 0 2 0 0 1 1 ,
  0 2 2 ⟶ }

Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
  Here, ↑ marks so-called defined symbols.
After renaming modulo the bijection { (1,↑) ↦ 0, (0,↓) ↦ 1, (0,↑) ↦ 2, (2,↓) ↦ 3, (1,↓) ↦ 4 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 8-rules system (5 strict rules)
{ 0 1 ⟶ 2 3 1 1 4 4 ,
  0 1 ⟶ 2 1 4 4 ,
  0 1 ⟶ 2 4 4 ,
  0 1 ⟶ 0 4 ,
  0 1 ⟶ 0 ,
  1 →= ,
  4 1 →= 1 3 1 1 4 4 ,
  1 3 3 →= }
